"Transport quantities not necessarily accurate. Better data may become available in the near future.; 51 objects show use wear. These were used on semi-soft and semi-hard materials. Cutting was mostly done on semi-soft materials (15 instances), although 3 instances of cutting was identified on semi-hard materials. Scraping action was identified on semi-soft materials on 12 occasions, while on semi-hard materials it was done in 7 occasions. 'Thinning' was identified in 8 instances on semi-soft, and 5 times on semi-hard materials. Unretouched objects that show cutting activity were used mostly on semi-soft material (10 vs. 1 on semi-hard), whilst the unretouched objects showing thinning action were used on both semi-hard and semi-soft materials equally (3 instances). Only one unretouched object showing scraping was identifed, which was used on semi-soft material. Retouched objects showing scraping were similarly mostly used on semi-soft materials (11 instances versus 7 on semi-hard). Both retouched objects associated with thinning and cutting were identified as been used on semi-soft material on 5 occasions, as opposed to 2 times on semi-hard material. One retouched object showing scraping could not be identified as being worked on any specific material."	"Lithics: Raynal, J.-P., Fernandes, P., Le Corre-Le Beux, M., and Santagata, C., 2007.
